(sa) par /
tshe dpag med sgrub rgyal lugs kyi bla brgyud smon lam bcas la /
(ha) par /
rje nyid kyi zhabs brtan blo chen rgyal kun ma la /
(a) par /
ka 'phreng dang sbyar ba'i mgur dbyangs la /
(A) par /
bla ma'i thugs rje bskul ba'i gdung dbyangs la /
(i) par /
mdo sngags lam gyi gnad don ching ba'i bskul dbyangs la /
(I) par /
stag phu mchog sprul rin po che'i zhabs brtan la /
(u) par /
dga' ldan the'u bo sprul sku'i zhabs brtan la /
(U) par /
khri chen ngag dbang nor bu'i rjes 'dzin 'dod gsol smon tshig la /
(r-i) par /
dam pa'i bka' drin dran pa'i smon tshig la /
(r-I) par /
rje ngag dbang dge legs dpal bzang po'i myur byon la /
(l-i) par /
bslab bya bsdus pa thams cad mkhyen pa la zhes pa'i dbu can la /
(l-I) par /
'dod gsol smon tshig skor la /
rje ngag dbang dge legs dpal bzang po'i dgongs rdzogs skabs gsar bzhengs mi pham pa'i smon tshig /
rgyal kun mtshan mchog ma /
'jam dbyangs sras mchog ma /
zangs mdog dpal dir /
rgyal kun snying rje ma /
'di bcas a tsa mchog sprul gyis /
gdugs dkar zhal thang dang /
zangs ri zhing bkod bcas kyi smon tshig /
yang des zhus pa'i /
'di bzhengs dge bas zhes tshigs bcad gcig /
sgrol ma 'jigs pa brgyad skyobs kyi smon tshig /
phyogs bcu rgyal kun ma /
rje dI baM ka ra'i snang brnyan gsar bzhengs kyi smon tshig /
grangs med rgyal ba ma /
(e) 'di phyi dge ba'i smon tshig skyabs gnas rin chen ma /
(ai) mgon po'i gtor chog mdor bsdus la /
(o) drug cu ma las bzhi'i 'bul tshul la /
(au) rgyal ba'i bstan srung gtso bo rnams la mchod gtor bskang 'phrin mdor bsdus las bzhi'i bang mdzod la /
(aM) bstan srung 'ga'i mchod gtor 'bul tshul legs tshogs lhun grub /
(aH) thu me yul gyi gzhi bdag gi gsol mchod bskang bshags tshogs bstod kyi kha skong dang bcas pa /
(ki) gnyal dang rgyal dgon gyi bka' srung rnam gsum gyi gtor 'bul la /

(khu) @# / /
mong gol cha gar yul gyi gzhi bdag gi bsang gsol bya tshul dgos pa kun 'grub la /
bka' 'gyur skabs gsung rgyu'i smon tshig bcas legs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni /
mdzad pa po lho sprul ngag dbang mkhyen rab bstan pa'i dbang phyug dpal bzang po /
des bdag la'o / /
! / /
gong sa rgyal dbang thams cad mkhyen gzigs chen po'i rigs kyi cod pan mkhan chen yongs 'dzin rdo rje 'chang chen po'i gsung 'bum ji ltar mnos pa'i mtshan byang bkod par /
dga' ldan lha brgya ma'i khrid yig man ngag gang+gA'i chu rgyun babs pa'i zegs ma /
rgyal dbang 'phrin las rgya mtsho la brten pa'i bla ma'i rnal 'byor nyams su len tshul byin rlabs bdud rtsi'i bum bzang /
rgyal dbang thams cad mkhyen gzigs rje btsun ngag dbang blo bzang thub bstan rgya mtsho la brten pa'i bla ma'i rnal 'byor byin rlabs bdud rtsi'i bum bzang /
rje tsong kha pa la brten pa'i bla ma'i rnal 'byor byin rlabs gru char 'bebs pa'i sprin sgra /
rje gzigs pa lnga ldan gyi bla ma'i rnal 'byor dad pa'i kun+da 'dzum byed /
'khor dag pa rnam brgyad kyi gsol 'debs 'gor rtsub reg dri bral zhes yod pa /
jo bo rje la brten pa'i bla ma'i rnal 'byor ldan ma yon tan dar rgyas nas zhus pa /
'phags pa thogs med nas bsgrub dus kyi byams pa la brten pa'i bla ma'i rnal 'byor rgyal sras spyod pa'i 'byung gnas /
byams pa'i bla ma'i rnal 'byor mi pham dgyes bskyed /
rje btsun byams pa'i gsol 'debs dge legs kun 'byung /
byams pa la brten pa'i bla ma'i rnal 'byor byin rlabs myur 'jug /
rje btsun 'jam dbyangs la brten pa'i bla ma'i rnal 'byor byin rlabs 'od stong 'dren pa'i shing rta /
thugs rje chen po'i rnal 'byor nyams su len tshul byin rlabs bdud rtsi'i thig 'phreng /
thugs rje chen po la brten pa'i bla ma'i rnal 'byor byin rlabs sprin phung /
sgrol dkar bla ma'i rnal 'byor 'chi med mchog stsol /
gsang 'dus la brten pa'i bla ma'i rnal 'byor dge legs bstan 'dzin ye shes chos bzang nas zhus pa /
'khor lo sdom par brten pa'i bla ma'i rnal 'byor mchog thun dngos grub 'gugs pa'i lcags kyu /
'jigs byed la brten pa'i bla ma'i rnal 'byor stag ring bla ma rin chen nas zhus pa /
kun rig bla ma'i rnal 'byor ldan ma 'bum dgon dge slong bshad sgrub rgyal mtshan nas zhus pa /
kun rig bla ma'i rnal 'byor 'gor bla ma lha la phyag 'tshal lo /
bcom ldan 'das kun rig rnam par snang mdzad kyi sgrub thabs nyams su len par 'dod pas zhes yod pa /
rje btsun 'jam dbyangs la brten pa'i bla ma'i rnal 'byor rnam grwa'i dge tshul byams pa skal ldan nas zhus pa /
rje btsun rdo rje rnal 'byor ma la brten pa'i bla ma'i rnal 'byor ldan @# / /
ma 'bum sgang grwa rigs dge slong skal bzang mthar phyin nas zhus pa /
yang de'i bla ma'i rnal 'byor 'gor rang gi snying gar pad nyi ru zhes yod pa /
bla ma dang rta mchog yang gsang khros pa dbyer med kyi rnal 'byor byin rlabs 'dod rgu'i mchog stsol /
bla ma'i rnal 'byor 'dren mchog bla ma dgyes byed mchod sprin /
zab lam bla ma'i rnal 'byor rgyud smad pa dge slong byams pa skal bzang dang blo bzang tshe brtan bcas nas zhus pa /
brag nag sprul skur gnang ba'i zab lam bla ma'i rnal 'byor /
bla ma'i rnal 'byor dngos grub kun 'byung /
bla ma'i rnal 'byor byin rlabs myur du 'gugs pa'i pho nya /

'khrul 'khor thig (a) rtsa le tshan (a) gnyis /
rgyal mtshan 'khor lo'i (a) cho (a) ga /
dus 'khor mdun bskyed phyi rol mchod (a) pa bum bskyed mdor bsdus (a) bcas mnos pa las rtags med rnams kyi ljags lung gi brgyud pa ni /
mdzad pa po rdzong dkar pa rje 'jigs med bsam gtan /
rje 'jam dbyangs thub bstan rgya mtsho /
bka' drin mtshungs med rje blo bzang lung rtogs bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po /

g.yung drung rtags can gyi brgyud pa ni /

yang a rtags can rnams kyi brgyud pa ni /
mdzad pa po nyid las thob / /
bde rtags can rnams kyi brgyud pa ni /
mdzad pa bo grub dbang 'jigs med bsam gtan /
bka' drin mtshungs med bde yang rje snyan grags rgya mtsho dpal bzang po'i zhal snga nas bdag la'o / /

rab byams rgyal ba kun gyi mkhyen rab gcig tu bsdus pa'i rang gzugs bka' drin mnyam med rdo rje 'chang rje btsun dge 'dun bstan 'dzin rgya mtsho dpal bzang bo'i gsung 'bum las lung mnos pa'i mtshan byang dang brgyud rim bcas dgod pa la /
byang chub bde lam gyi khrid dmigs skyong tshul shin tu gsal (ra) bar bkod pa dge legs 'od snang 'byed pa'i nyin byed la /
rigs dang dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho'i mnga' bdag rje btsun blo bzang lung rigs rgya mtsho dpal bzang po'i rnam thar dad ldan rna ba'i bcud len la /
rje btsun bcom ldan 'das ma rig byed ma la brten pa'i tshe'i dngos grub sgrub (ra) pa'i cho ga dge legs chu gter spel ba'i zla shel la /
khyad bdag 'khor lo'i mgon po rje btsun blo bzang bstan pa'i dbang phyug tshul khrims phun tshogs dpal bzang po'i rnam thar kun (ra) bzang spyod tshul gsal ba'i me long la /
sku gsung thugs rten gsar bzhengs kyi dkar chag dang zhal byang par smon bshad pa 'ga' nyung bcas phyogs bsdebs su bkod pa bde legs dgos 'dod kun stsol nor bu'i bang mdzod las shog grangs gya bdun pa yan /
bshes gnyen dam pa'i rjes 'dzin smon tshig sgor 'dod rgu'i gru char 'jo ba'i sprin phung las shog grangs bcu gnyis pa'i brnyes dbon po'i rjes 'dzin yan /
skyes chen dam pa rnams kyi yang sprul myur byon gsol 'debs @# / /
skor nyam chung yid kyi gsos sman las shog grangs nyer gcig pa'i lo kyA zhabs drung gi myur byon gsol 'debs yan /
lhag lha du ma'i 'dod gsol brgyud 'debs smon lam sna tshogs phyogs gcig tu bkod pa byin rlabs nor bu'i gter mdzod las shog grangs bcu gnyis pa yan /
skyes chen dam pa rnams kyi zhabs brtan gsol 'debs skor drang srong rgan po'i bden tshig las shog grangs bcu gnyis pa yan /
rang gzhan chos la bskul ba'i mgur dbyangs kyi rim pa phyogs gcig tu bkod pa skal bzang yid kyi gdung sel las shog grangs bdun pa yan la| blo sbyong tshigs brgyad ma'i zin bris (ra) skal bzang spyi nor la /
lta khrid dran pa bzhi ldan gyi zin bris (ra) legs bshad rin thang med pa'i rgyan la /
me tog bcud len gyi zin bris mdor bsdus dka' (ra) thub spyod ba'i rgyan la /
rngog dkyil bdun las ma rgyud dkyil 'khor drug dang (ra) rdor dbyings kyi dbang gi brjed byang gdung sel bdud rtsi'i khrus rdzing la /
'khor chen gyi brgyud 'debs dang smon shis mdor bsdus (ra) la /
dpal 'khor lo chen po'i sgrub thabs bdud sde zil gyis gnon pa'i bzhad sgra la /
snyan ngag me long las byung ba'i rgyan rnams kyi dper brjod legs bshad (ra) bdud rtsi'i mchod yon la /
bcas kyi lung brgyud ni /
rab byams rgyal kun 'dus pa'i bdag nyid 'jam mgon bstan pa'i snang byed mtshungs med bka' drin gzhal las 'das pa rje btsun bstan 'dzin rgya mtsho /
kun sangs 'dul 'dzin dbang po dkon mchog phun tshogs /
bka' drin mtshungs med rje blo bzang lung rtogs bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po /
des bdag la'o /

mkhas shing grub pa'i dbang phyug khya dge dpon slob rin po che blo gros rgya mtsho dpal bzang po'i gsung 'bum po ti gcig gi lung thob pa'i rim pa ni /
rje btsun bla ma dam pa'i rnam thar skal ldan re skong la /
rnam thar zur 'debs mjug bsdus dang bcas pa sgom chen blo bzang bkra shis kyis mdzad pa la lung med /
rje bla ma blo gros rgya mtsho'i gsang ba'i rnam thar pad dkar phreng ba sogs chos skyong gis mdzad pa le tshan 'ga' la lung med /
'jam dbyangs dmar ser la brten pa'i bla ma'i rnal 'byor byin rlabs myur 'jug /
gsol 'debs don gnyis lhun grub /
bla ma dang rigs gsum tha mi dad kyi gsol 'debs blo gros rab yangs ma /
gsol 'debs rigs kun khyab bdag ma sogs la /
yan lag bdun pa rab mchog rgyal ba ma /
'jigs byed kyi gsol @# / /
'debs gang drin ma /
'jigs byed la bstod pa ka phreng ma /
rta mgrin la bstod pa ka phreng ma /
mgon po zhal bzhi pa'i bstod pa ka phreng ma /
mgon po phyag drug pa'i bstod pa ka phreng ma rnams la /
skyes bu gsum gyi lam rnam par nges pa bya dka' ba'i mdzes rgyan gyi 'grel ba gsal ba'i sgron me la /
gsung mgur /
rje gsum ldan ma /
rgyal ba kun dngos ma /
gnas dben pa ma /
gsum ldan dam pa ma /
skyabs gnas kun 'dus ma /
rje rdo rje 'chang dbang ma /
paN chen thams cad mkhyen pa dran pa'i gsol 'debs ka lA pa Na zhes pa'i dbu can /
skyabs gnas kun 'dus ma /
gsum ldan bka' drin ma rnams la /
dge tshul gyi blang dor phyin ci ma log par ston pa'i bslab bya cung zad bsdus pa slob ma la phan pa la /
byang chub sems dpa'i ltung ba bshags pa'i 'grel ba la /
klu dbang rgyal po'i sgrub thabs /
'jigs byed zhe dgu ma'i rgyu'i lha zhe dgu'i lung sbyor /
rgyud sde 'og ma'i lugs kyi ma Ni ril sgrub /
bsang chu sgrub tshul /
gsang bdag gos sngon can gyi sgrub thabs rnams la /
dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi sgrub thabs za ma tog gi rnam bshad thar 'dod 'jug dogs la /
dpal 'khor lo bde mchog lU i pa'i bskyed rim skal ldan re skong dang /
bde mchog rtsa sngags kyi nges don kyi bshad pa sogs la /
mgon po'i gtor 'bul 'jigs rung ma /
rnam sras gtor 'bul byang phyogs lcang lo ma /
mgon chos lha mo gsum gyi bzlas dmigs mdor bsdus /
gnyer gtad mgon po spyan ras gzigs dbang ma /
rje gsum ldan ma /
rgyal pa'i yum mchog ma /
bla ma yi dam rnams la /
bsangs yig chos dbyings ma /
bsangs yig dngos grub kun 'byung ma /
brag dkar gyi bsangs yig 'phrin las kun 'grub rnams la /
bsngo ba tshigs lhug ma /
bsngo ba tshigs bcad mang po 'gro ba'i 'dren mchog ma /
bsngo ba 'dir 'bad rnam dkar ma /
bsngo ba phun tshogs dge legs ma /
bsngo ba phyogs bcur bzhugs pa'i ma rnams la /
khyon bsdoms bcas bzhugs /
de rnams kyi lung mnos pa'i brgyud pa ni /

sgom chen blo bzang bkra shis /
'dul 'dzin kha rdo gnas brtan blo bzang bstan 'dzin /
'dul 'dzin 'jam dbyangs shes rab| rab 'byams pa ngag dbang bsam grub /

lcang lung khri rgan 'jam dbyangs thub bstan rgya mtsho dpal bzang po'i gsung 'bum gras bzhugs pa las /
'phags mchog thugs rje chen po phyag bzhi pa la brten pa'i ma Ni ril sgrub bya tshul byin rlabs char 'bebs nor bu'i phreng ba /
rong bo no min han mchog sprul rin po che blo bzang skal ldan bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa /
rigs gsum spyi sgrub kyi bdag bskyed rgyas bsdus nyam su len tshul dngos grub kun 'byung la /
thugs rje chen po tshem bu dmar khrid kyi rgyun khyer mdor bsdus nor bu padma'i zhal lung la /
rje btsun rig byed ma la brten pa'i g.yang 'bod dang 'dod gsol nor bu don yod lcags kyu /
'jam dbyangs zhi khro sbrags sgrub kyi man ngag thun mong ba dag 'don bklag chog dri med shes rab mig 'byed la /
myur mdzad ye shes kyi mgon po phyag drug pa'i gtor chog mdor bsdus dngos grub bum bzang la /
bslab bya snying gtam bcu gsum snying gi ri mo mtshon byed la /
zab don gcod kyi gdams pa phaT bdun mar grags pa'i khrid yig mdor bsdus gnad don kun gsal nor bu'i sgron me la /
grub dbang gnyan tshem bu lugs kyi thugs rje chen po phyag bzhi pa'i zhi ba'i sbyin sreg bklags pas don 'grub la /
gnyan tshem bu pa'i lugs kyi thugs rje chen po'i sgrub thabs sogs thor bu 'ga' zhig la /
ma cig khros ma nag mo lha lnga'i sgrub thabs dngos grub mdzod kyi lde mig la /
smyung gnas dang 'brel bar bcu gcig zhal gyi bsnyen pa byed tshul dngos grub mchog sbyin la /
yul khyad par can la lha bshos 'bul tshul /
bcom ldan 'das rig pa'i rgyal po 'jam dpal nA ga rak+Sha'i zhi ba'i sbyin sreg bdud rtsi'i bum bzang la /
so sor thar ba'i sdom pa gtan la dbab pa 'dul ba rgya mtsho'i snying po bsdus pa'i tshig 'grel padma dkar po'i chun po la /
grub dbang tshem bu lugs kyi thugs rje chen po phyag bzhi pa'i bsnyen yig dngos grub 'dod 'jo la /
rje btsun 'phags ma sgrol ma la brten nas gter sgrub bya tshul dngos grub gru char g.yo ba'i sprin phung la /
dzam dkar gter sgrub bsdus pa dngos grub mdzod kyi lnge mig la /
dzam dkar lha lnga'i gter sgrub bya tshul shin tu khyer bde bar bkod pa dngos grub gru char g.yo ba'i sprin phung la / /
stag phu sgrol ma'i @# / /
zhi rgyas dbang gsum gyi 'khor lo sgrub pa'i cho ga gsal bar bkod pa dgos 'dod kun 'byung /
rje btsun sgrol ma'i rnal 'byor pa 'ga' zhig gis grub pa brgyad sgrub ma dgos par grub pa'i lo rgyas lha'i rol mo /
dza bIr gyi rlung khrid 'ja' lus mngon gyur ngag dbang phun tshogs kyis zin bris su btab pa /
dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed ser po la brten nas tshe'i dngos grub sgrub pa'i cho ga 'chi med bdud rtsi'i bcud len la /
bcas gong gsal de rnams kyi ljags lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni /
mdzad pa po 'jam dbyangs thub bstan rgya mtsho /
a rol rin po che rje blo bzang lung rtogs bstan pa'i rgya mtshan dpal bzang po /
